        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1866753461" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17604233771182838212">Damn! This had everything I ever need in a fantasy novel.<br/>- Intricate yet understandable magic system<br/>- Original world building<br/>- Little to no romance<br/>- Solid evil villains<br/>- Fantastic characters with humour<br/>- Addictive storyline<br/><br/>Guys I absolutely adored this, and how has it taken me this long to read?<br/>Writing this, I cannot think of even 1 think I disliked. <br/><br/>Kell is an <i>Antari</i> someone with magic powers, able to travel between the 4 Londons. Red - his home, Grey - the dull London where magic is nearly all</span>
  <span id="freeText17604233771182838212" style="display:none">Damn! This had everything I ever need in a fantasy novel.<br />- Intricate yet understandable magic system<br />- Original world building<br />- Little to no romance<br />- Solid evil villains<br />- Fantastic characters with humour<br />- Addictive storyline<br /><br />Guys I absolutely adored this, and how has it taken me this long to read?<br />Writing this, I cannot think of even 1 think I disliked. <br /><br />Kell is an <i>Antari</i> someone with magic powers, able to travel between the 4 Londons. Red - his home, Grey - the dull London where magic is nearly all gone and White - where magic is controlled and used to assume power, and once there was a Black London, consumed and destroyed.<br /><br />When Kell becomes tangled up in some dark magic, he takes it upon himself to make it right. Along with Lila Bard - a thief and cut-throat he just can't seem to shake. <br /><br />I loved this. I don't know what else to say. This was my first Schwab book, but it absolutely will not be my last! Roll on book 2! :) <br /><br /><br />****************************************************<br /><br />Outstanding!!!!</span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/69838582-theburqaavenger?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>,

          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2312481139" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4307964089495559918"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"For the ones who dream of stranger worlds"</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1592913661i/29694290._SY540_.jpg' width='1000' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>"A Darker Shade of Magic" was my first book by V.E. Schwab and i had really high expectations while going into this story and let me just say i was not disappointed. This book totally deserves all the hype because it was <b>unique, powerful and enchanting</b>. The writing style and the world building gripped me from the beginning and i literally flew through this book. The story was well paced and i absolutely loved our narrators. But the true magi</span>
  <span id="freeText4307964089495559918" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"For the ones who dream of stranger worlds"</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1592913661i/29694290._SY540_.jpg" width="1000" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>"A Darker Shade of Magic" was my first book by V.E. Schwab and i had really high expectations while going into this story and let me just say i was not disappointed. This book totally deserves all the hype because it was <b>unique, powerful and enchanting</b>. The writing style and the world building gripped me from the beginning and i literally flew through this book. The story was well paced and i absolutely loved our narrators. But the true magic of this book was well in its <b>magic</b>.<br>And this book did have some liabilities due to which i ducked out a star but we will talk about it in the end because <b>this book was too close to perfect to waste our time on brooding about its negatives</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"I'd rather die on an adventure than live standing still."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><u>
  <b>The World-Building</b>
</u><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Sure I do,” countered Lila cheerfully. “There’s Dull London, Kell London, Creepy London, and Dead London,” she recited, ticking them off on her fingers. “See? I’m a fast learner"</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1592913661i/29694291._SY540_.jpg" width="1000" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The World-Building was absolutely <i>amazing</i>. It was so unique and it had such an element of distinction. Four londons separated by doors which only special people <i>Antari</i> can cross? Woah. Everytime Kell told us about the Londons i sat at the edge of my seat gripping my book tightly, willing the book to change its words because <i>i could totally read volumes about the world the author has created</i>. <br>I felt like i was with Kell when he went to Grey London and I could feel the dullness of that place. I could feel the horror of White London and I cannot wait to learn more about this world.<br><br><u>
  <b>The Magic</b>
</u><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Magic bent the world. Pulled it into shape."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1592915133i/29694630._SY540_.jpg" width="1000" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br><br>The magical system was absolutely enthralling. I for one was amazed by the brilliance of the author. She kept pulling me back into the world by introducing new things and it was so <i>perfectly balanced</i>. I couldn't decide who was right about the magic. Kell who insists on treating magic like an equal? Or Holland who says that a person should be a master of something to control it?<br>By introducing a completely new language for the magic and by providing an enchanting backstory of the magic, the author had me hooked throughout the whole book.<br><br><u>
  <b>The Pacing</b>
</u><br><br>I know a lot of people don't care about the pacing but for me it is one of the most important elements and trust me when i say this <i>i was not bored</i>. Not for a single moment. There is such an <i>eveness</i> throughout the book.<br><br><u>
  <b>The Characters</b>
</u><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1592913661i/29694293._SX540_.jpg" width="1000" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Kell</b> and <b>Lila</b> were a perfect pair. I loved reading about their adventures and how they were so different yet so similar to each other<br><br><b>Rhy</b> was not given much book time but i loved him so much i really hope the author further explores his and Kell's relationship because I was totally enamored by their relation and he was such a sweetheart.<br> <br>Everytime <b>Holland</b> appeared i wanted to cover my windows because *shivers*. He was an absolutely perfect villain.<br><br><b>The Dane Twins</b>.......They drink your milkshake guys.<br><br><u>
  <b>The Coat</b>
</u><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Kell wore a very peculiar coat. It had neither one side, which would be conventional, nor two, which would be unexpected, but several, which was, of course, impossible."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1592913661ra/29694294.gif" width="1000" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Yes the coat because it was a <i>perfect stroke of genius</i> and I have an otp now:<br><blockquote>Me+ The Coat= OTP forever</blockquote><br><br><u>
  <b>The Fights</b>
</u><br><br>They were the <i>highlight of this book for me</i>. It gave <i>A:TLA</i> vibes. And i was shaking with anticipation about what would happen next.<br><br><u>
  <b>The Cons</b>
</u><br><br>Firstly, the whole story felt <i>too centered on Kell and Lila</i>. It depended too much on only their choices. We were reading about <i>four londons</i> but still every single thing depended on those two.<br>Secondly, <i>every minor character in the story was introduced just for the mere fact that they could be killed</i> and so that Kell and Lila could live. At the end of this book i did a mental tally and there is not a single minor character left alive and those that are left alive I assure you they will play the role of secondary characters in the next book.<br><br><u>
  <b>Conclusion</b>
</u><br><br>This was an amazing book and I am so glad I picked it up!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1592913661i/29694295._SY540_.jpg" width="1000" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And I am not going to die until I have read every book by V.E. Schwab.</span>
  <a data-text-id="4307964089495559918" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('VvuuWlcSPOh2DmsdfuEMxdcO4sp92L8QHlKz9gZgQt01om6E17fgOfcaa4pz7l57v953nul9d5886BhFSfaUiA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('Kt/q14a4hn+0PQgqSBSxqsay586g9gJN+rdcehrJwQ5JhioJBh1arjUpCL1FG+MUrmJymjRTysLYDffJVV8XWw==')})
  }
